#226
country_event = {
	id = jap.1
	title = jap.1.t
	desc = jap.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_officers

	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = JAP
		has_government = fascism
		date > 1936.2.25
		date < 1939.1.1
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 85
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 60
			}
		}
		name = jap.1.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = -0.40
		}
		add_ideas = JAP_toseiha_idea
		hidden_effect = {
			add_country_leader_trait = JAP_toseiha_trait
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 15
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = no
				factor = 40
			}
		}
		name = jap.1.b
		set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_kodoha name = JAP_kodoha }
		set_party_name = { ideology = neutrality long_name = JAP_toseiha name = JAP_toseiha }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = -0.40
		}
		add_ideas = JAP_kodoha_idea
		hidden_effect = {
			add_country_leader_trait = JAP_kodoha_trait
		}
	}
}

#taiseiyokusankai
country_event = {
	id = jap.2
	title = jap.2.t
	desc = jap.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_government = fascism
		fascism > 0.7
		date > 1940.10.6
	}
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 6 }
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_taiseiyokusankai name = JAP_taiseiyokusankai }
		}
		set_country_flag = taiseiyokusankai
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.2.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_party_name = { ideology = fascism long_name = JAP_taiseiyokusankai name = JAP_taiseiyokusankai }
		}
	}
}

#establish pgr?
country_event = {
	id = jap.3
	title = jap.3.t
	desc = jap.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_parade

	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = JAP
		has_government = fascism
		has_offensive_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		608 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
				has_offensive_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				has_full_control_of_state = 608
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			country_exists = PGR
			has_global_flag = is_1939_start
			PGR = {
				has_country_flag = bridge_choose_die
			}
			has_war_together_with = HYQ
		}
	}
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 6 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		PGR = {
			add_state_claim = 609
			add_state_claim = 608
			add_state_claim = 614
			add_state_claim = 597
			add_state_claim = 615
			add_state_claim = 795
			transfer_state = 608
			set_capital = { state = 608 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						PRC = {
							has_completed_focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
						}
					}
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								PRC = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
										progress > 0.75
									}
								}
							}
							else = {
								if = {
									limit = {
										PRC = {
											focus_progress = {
												focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
												progress > 0.50
											}
										}
									}
									else = {
										if = {
											limit = {
												PRC = {
													focus_progress = {
														focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
														progress > 0.25
													}
												}
											}
											else = {
												if = {
													limit = {
														PRC = {
															focus_progress = {
																focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
																progress > 0
															}
														}
													}
												}
											}
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = PGR
				autonomous_state = autonomy_puppet
			}
		}
		EHA = {
			country_event = { id = jap.4 days = 1 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			PGR = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					relation = military_access
					country = MEN
					active = yes
				}
				MEN = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						relation = military_access
						country = PGR
						active = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = RGR
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						relation = military_access
						country = RGR
						active = yes
					}
					RGR = {
						diplomatic_relation = {
							relation = military_access
							country = PGR
							active = yes
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = "PGR_established"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
						capital_scope = {
							state = 608
						}
					}
				}
				event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
					set_country_flag = capital_in_enemy_puppet
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.3.b
	}
}

#get absorbed by pgr?
country_event = {
	id = jap.4
	title = jap.4.t
	desc = jap.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_parade

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.4.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		EHA = {
			remove_state_core = 609
		}
		PGR = {
			annex_country = { target = EHA transfer_troops = yes }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.4.b
		JAP = {
			end_puppet = EHA
			declare_war_on = {
				target = EHA
				type = annex_everything
			}
		}
		EHA = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 80
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = neutrality
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				ZZZ = {
					EHA_zhang_yantian = { set_nationality = EHA }
					EHA_zhang_qingyu = { set_nationality = EHA }
				}
				JAP = {
					country_event = { id = jap.5 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#tungchow mutiny
country_event = {
	id = jap.6
	title = jap.6.t
	desc = jap.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_dead_soldiers

	trigger = {
		tag = EHA
		JAP = {
			has_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		}
	}
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_country_leader = yes
			add_manpower = -220
			609 = {
				add_manpower = -220
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = { id = jap.7 }
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = EHA
					modifier = tungchow_mutiny
				}
			}
			EHA_chi_zongmo = { promote_character = { ideology = fascism_ideology }}
		}
	}
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.6.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			add_manpower = -220
			609 = {
				add_manpower = -220
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				name = "Ch'ih Tzung-mo"
				ideology = fascism_ideology
			}
		}
	}
}

#establish rgr?
country_event = {
	id = jap.8
	title = jap.8.t
	desc = jap.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_parade

	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = JAP
		has_government = fascism
		has_offensive_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		613 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
				has_offensive_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				has_full_control_of_state = 613
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			RGR = { exists = yes }
			has_global_flag = is_1939_start
			has_war_together_with = HYQ
		}
	}
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 6 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		RGR = {
			add_state_claim = 596
			add_state_claim = 796
			add_state_claim = 606
			add_state_claim = 613
			add_state_claim = 598
			add_state_claim = 794
			transfer_state = 613
			set_capital = { state = 613 }
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						PRC = {
							has_completed_focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
						}
					}
					add_ideas = PRC_enemy_partisan
					else = {
						if = {
							limit = {
								PRC = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
										progress > 0.75
									}
								}
							}
							add_ideas = PRC_enemy_partisan_4
						}else_if = {
							limit = {
								PRC = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
										progress > 0.50
									}
								}
							}
							add_ideas = PRC_enemy_partisan_3
						}else_if = {
							limit = {
								PRC = {
									focus_progress = {
										focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
										progress > 0.25
									}
								}
							}
							add_ideas = PRC_enemy_partisan_2
						}else = {
							if = {
								limit = {
									PRC = {
										focus_progress = {
											focus = PRC_front_line_behind_enemy_line
											progress > 0
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = {
			set_autonomy = {
				target = RGR
				autonomous_state = autonomy_puppet
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			RGR = {
				diplomatic_relation = {
					relation = military_access
					country = MEN
					active = yes
				}
				MEN = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						relation = military_access
						country = RGR
						active = yes
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = PGR
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						relation = military_access
						country = PGR
						active = yes
					}
					PGR = {
						diplomatic_relation = {
							relation = military_access
							country = RGR
							active = yes
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						country_exists = EHA
					}
					diplomatic_relation = {
						relation = military_access
						country = EHA
						active = yes
					}
					EHA = {
						diplomatic_relation = {
							relation = military_access
							country = RGR
							active = yes
						}
					}
				}
				load_oob = "RGR_established"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
						capital_scope = {
							state = 613
						}
					}
				}
				event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
					set_country_flag = capital_in_enemy_puppet
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.3.b
	}
}

#install wangjingwei?
country_event = {
	id = jap.9
	title = jap.9.t
	desc = jap.9.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_asian_politicians

	trigger = {
		always = no
		tag = JAP
		has_government = fascism
		has_offensive_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
		613 = {
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
				has_offensive_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				has_full_control_of_state = 613
			}
		}
		country_exists = PGR
		country_exists = RGR
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
		}
		PGR = {
			is_puppet_of = JAP
			has_capitulated = no
		}
		RGR = {
			is_puppet_of = JAP
			has_capitulated = no
		}
	}
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 290 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.3.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			effect_tooltip = {
				start_civil_war = {
					ideology = fascism
					capital = 613
				}
			}
		} 
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = jap.10 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = man_puppet_wjw_tt
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.3.b
	}
}

#setup wjw
country_event = {
	id = jap.10
	hidden = yes
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = WJW_established
		JAP = { 
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dlc = "Waking the Tiger"
				}
				JAP = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = WJW
						autonomous_state = autonomy_wtt_imperial_protectorate
					}
				}
				else = {
					if = {
						limit = {
							has_dlc = "Together for Victory"
						}
						JAP = {
							set_autonomy = {
								target = WJW
								autonomous_state = autonomy_integrated_puppet
							}
						}
						else = {
							JAP = {
								set_autonomy = {
									target = WJW
									autonomous_state = autonomy_puppet
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = RGR
					tag = PGR
					tag = ECR
					tag = EHA
					is_chinese_nations_w_HYQ = yes
				}
				NOT = {
					tag = SIK
					tag = NSM
					tag = XSM
					tag = MEN
				}
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
			country_event = { id = jap.125 }
		}
		event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
			country_event = { id = jap.145 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
	}
}

#puyi coronation
country_event = {
	id = jap.11
	title = jap.11.t
	desc = jap.11.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_journalists_speech

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.11.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		ROOT = {
			declare_war_on = {
				target = FROM
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_other_country = {
						has_war_with = ROOT
						is_major = yes
						strength_ratio = {
							tag = ROOT
							ratio > 1.25
						}
					}
				}
				add = 60
			}
		}
		name = jap.11.b
		add_political_power = -250
		add_stability = -0.1
	}
}

#usa ultimatum
country_event = {
	id = jap.17
	title = jap.17.t
	desc = jap.17.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		#anchor: MAN gain independence
		name = jap.17.a
		set_global_flag = JAP_grant_MAN_independence
		MAN = { 
			set_country_flag = MAN_free_flag 
			capital_scope = {
				if = {
					limit = { NOT = { has_state_flag = MAN_state_secured }}
					add_to_variable = { global.MAN_secured_state_num = 1 }
					set_state_flag = MAN_state_secured
					custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_state_secured_tt
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 10
		}
		end_puppet = MAN
		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = MAN }
			remove_from_faction = MAN
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = jap.19 }
			diplomatic_relation = { relation = guarantee country = MAN active = yes }
		}
		MAN = {
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = MAN_assimilated_bandits
					is_core_of = ROOT
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAN_local_bandits }
					NOT = {
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAN_najua_presence }
						has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAN_najua_presence2 }
					}
				}
				if = { limit = { has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAN_local_bandits }} remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = MAN_local_bandits }}
				if = { limit = { has_resistance = yes } cancel_resistance = yes }
				if = { limit = { check_variable = { global.MAN_resistance_strength@This> 0 }} set_variable = { global.MAN_resistance_strength@This= 0 }}
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_war_with = ROOT 
					OR = {
						is_faction_leader = yes
						is_in_faction = no
					}
					NOT = { 
						tag = PREV
						is_in_faction_with = PREV
						is_subject_of = PREV
						OVERLORD = { is_in_faction_with = PREV }
					}
					NOT = { tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag }
				}
				country_event = { id = jap.222 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = neutrality
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = neutrality
					elections_allowed = no
					last_election = "1936.1.1"
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = neutrality
				popularity = 0.5
			}
			set_variable = { MAN_awareness = 0 }
			set_variable = { MAN_suspicion = 0 }
			set_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood = 0 }
			country_event = { id = jap.20 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MAN_korean_cooperation_flag
			}
			if = {
				limit = { KOR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }}
				end_puppet = KOR
				if = {
					limit = { KOR = { has_war = yes }}
					hidden_effect = { KOR = { country_event = { id = wd.1 }} }
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
						}
					}
					is_core_of = KOR
				}
				KOR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		#TODO news
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.17.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 90
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 0.5
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = jap.21 }
			declare_war_on = {
				target = ROOT
				type = topple_government
			}
		}
	}
}

		always = no
	}

			random_owned_controlled_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = MAN
					free_building_slots = {
						building = industrial_complex
						size > 2
						include_locked = yes
					}
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				set_state_flag = MAN_xt_1
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.37.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			random_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = MAN_xt_1
				}
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#rfp request to fight soviet
country_event = {
	id = jap.47
	title = jap.47.t
	desc = jap.47.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_stalin_propaganda
	
	trigger = {
		tag = MAN
		is_puppet = no
		exists = yes
		has_idea = MAN_rfr_supporters
		has_capitulated = no
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = JAP
			has_war_with = SOV
			has_war_together_with = SOV
		}
		SOV = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = fascism
			}
			has_civil_war = no
		}
	}
	
	#is_triggered_only = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 90 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.47.a
		SOV = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = fascism
				capital = 408
				states = { 408 409 560 657 655 537 561 563 }
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SOV
				has_government = fascism
			}
			create_faction = rfp_white_movement
			add_to_faction = MAN
			MAN = {
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = PREV
					enemy = SOV
				}
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = MAN_RFP_white_movement
				days = 1700
			}
			add_ideas = {
				service_by_requirement
				war_economy
				closed_economy
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = "RFP_anti_bolshelvik"
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = 12000 producer = MAN }
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = infantry_weapons
							NOT = {
								has_tech = infantry_weapons1
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 15500 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = infantry_weapons1
							NOT = {
								has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 15500 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
							NOT = {
								has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_2 amount = 15500 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_3 amount = 15500 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = gw_artillery
							NOT = {
								has_tech = artillery1
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_1 amount = 9000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = artillery1
							NOT = {
								has_tech = artillery4
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_2 amount = 9000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = artillery4
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_3 amount = 9000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = motorised_infantry
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = motorized_equipment_1 amount = 7500 producer = MAN }
				}
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = MAN_rfr_supporters
		hidden_effect = {
			408 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 8
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 5
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 5
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			563 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			409 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 6
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.47.b
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_10_t_prepare_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = jap.56 days = 366 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.47.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_rfp_rise_tt
		set_country_flag = MAN_deny_rfp_request
		remove_ideas = MAN_rfr_supporters
		hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = jap.49 days = 10 }}
	}
}

		set_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood = 0 }

			target = FROM
			type = topple_government
		}

					exists = yes
					is_subject = no

			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MAN_prepared_for_sov_intervention

					exists = yes

				}

#join usa!
country_event = {
	id = jap.61
	title = jap.22.t
	desc = jap.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_heavy_cruiser

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		tag = MAN
		USA = {
			has_war_with = JAP
		}
		is_puppet_of = JAP
		has_global_flag = MAN_will_join_usa
	}
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			MAN = {
				overlord = {
					set_autonomy = {
						target = MAN
						autonomy_state = autonomy_free
					}
				}
			}
			USA = {
				set_autonomy = {
					target = MAN
					autonomy_state = autonomy_puppet
				}
				set_autonomy = {
					target = MAN
					autonomy_state = autonomy_free
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction = no
					}
					create_faction = man_liberate
					add_to_faction = MAN
					else = {
						random_country = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									is_in_faction_with = USA
									tag = USA
								}
								is_faction_leader = yes
							}
							add_to_faction = MAN
						}
					}
				}
			}
			MAN = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = JAP
					type = take_core_state
					generator = { 745 }
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = democratic
					elections_allowed = no
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = communism
					popularity = 0
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 5
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 20
				}
				set_political_party = {
					ideology = democratic
					popularity = 80
				}
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = USA
					enemy = JAP
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				country_event = { id = jap.23 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.22.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			JAP = {
				end_puppet = MAN
			}
			add_to_war = {
				targeted_alliance = USA
				enemy = JAP
			}
		}
	}
}

#change to civil war
country_event = {
	id = jap.63
	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		original_tag = MAN
		has_war_with = SOV
	}
	
	immediate = {
		SOV = {
			start_civil_war = {
				ideology = fascism
				capital = 408
				states = { 408 409 560 657 655 537 561 563 }
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = {
				original_tag = SOV
				has_government = fascism
			}
			create_faction = rfp_white_movement
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = MAN_RFP_white_movement
				days = 1700
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = "RFP_anti_bolshelvik"
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
				load_oob = "RFP_anti_bolshelvik"
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = support_equipment_1 amount = 15000 producer = MAN }
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = infantry_weapons
							NOT = {
								has_tech = infantry_weapons1
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 25000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = infantry_weapons1
							NOT = {
								has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 25000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = improved_infantry_weapons
							NOT = {
								has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_2 amount = 25000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = advanced_infantry_weapons
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_3 amount = 25000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = gw_artillery
							NOT = {
								has_tech = artillery1
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_1 amount = 10000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = artillery1
							NOT = {
								has_tech = artillery4
							}
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_2 amount = 10000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = artillery4
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = artillery_equipment_3 amount = 10000 producer = MAN }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = {
							has_tech = motorised_infantry
						}
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = motorized_equipment_1 amount = 7500 producer = MAN }
				}
			add_ideas = war_economy
			add_ideas = service_by_requirement
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			408 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 8
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 5
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 5
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			563 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 3
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 2
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 1
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
			409 = {
				add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 6
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = infrastructure
					level = 3
					instant_build = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
	}

				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@KMT_central_gov_tag > 49 }
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@KMT_central_gov_tag > 89 }
				add = 100
			}
			modifier = {

				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@KMT_central_gov_tag > 49 }
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@KMT_central_gov_tag > 90 }
				add = 100
			}
		}
		name = jap.74.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = KMT_MEN_trigger_by_unify_focus
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.74.c
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				check_variable = { KMT_ps_loyalty@KMT_central_gov_tag > 70 }
				add = 10
			}

country_event = {
	id = jap.75
	title = jap.75.t
	desc = jap.75.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_chinese_soldiers_01
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.75.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		puppet = MEN
		MEN = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = ECR
				}
				annex_country = {
					target = ECR
					transfer_troops = yes
				}
				793 = {
					remove_core_of = ECR
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = fascism
					popularity = 1
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = neutrality
					popularity = 0.1
				}
				ECR = {
					every_unit_leader = { 
						#effect_tooltip = { set_nationality = ROOT }
						set_character_flag = KMT_temp_sn_flag
					}
					every_character = {
						limit = { has_character_flag = KMT_temp_sn_flag }
						set_nationality = HYQ
						clr_character_flag = KMT_temp_sn_flag
					}
				}
			}
				MEN_Yondonwangchug = { promote_character = { ideology = rexism }}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_government = fascism
					}
				}
				set_politics = {
					ruling_party = fascism
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = jap.76 }
			set_cosmetic_tag = MMGmen
			if = {
				limit = {
					JAP = {
						has_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
					}
				}
				add_to_war = {
					targeted_alliance = JAP
					enemy = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.75.b
		add_political_power = 25
		MEN = {
			country_event = { id = jap.77 }
		}
	}
}

			}

			}
		}
	}

country_event = {
	id = jap.108
	title = jap.108.t
	desc = jap.108.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_china_politicians_captured
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		any_country = {
			OR = {
				tag = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				tag = WJW
			}
			is_puppet_of = JAP
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				ECR = {
					exists = yes
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = ECR
					any_neighbor_state = {
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				RGR = {
					exists = yes
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = RGR
					any_neighbor_state = {
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				PGR = {
					exists = yes
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = PGR
					any_neighbor_state = {
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				EHA = {
					exists = yes
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = EHA
					any_neighbor_state = {
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		name = jap.108.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				PGR = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					exists = yes
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = PGR
					any_neighbor_state = {
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
			PGR = {
				country_event = { id = jap.123 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				RGR = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					exists = yes
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = RGR
					any_neighbor_state = {
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
			RGR = {
				country_event = { id = jap.123 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				EHA = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					exists = yes
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = EHA
					any_neighbor_state = {
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
			EHA = {
				country_event = { id = jap.123 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ECR = {
					is_puppet_of = JAP
					exists = yes
				}
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = ECR
					any_neighbor_state = {
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
			ECR = {
				country_event = { id = jap.123 }
			}
		}
	}

		name = jap.108.b
		add_political_power = -1
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = jap.111
	title = jap.111.t
	desc = jap.111.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_fascist_gathering
	
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				tag = JAP
				GER = { 
					NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
					NOT = { has_war_with = JAP }
					is_subject = no
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
			AND = {
				tag = GER
				JAP = { 
					NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
					NOT = { has_war_with = GER }
					is_subject = no
					has_government = fascism
				}
			}
		}
		has_war_with = SOV
		is_subject = no
		has_government = fascism
		has_global_flag = GER_JAP_tripartite_pact
		NOT = { has_global_flag = pending_join_against_sov_event }
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 3 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		set_global_flag = pending_join_against_sov_event
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100	
			modifier = {
				factor = 1
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = jap.111.a
		if = {
			limit = { tag = JAP }
			GER = { country_event = { id = jap.116 }}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = GER }
			JAP = { country_event = { id = jap.116 }}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				factor = 99
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		name = jap.111.b
		clr_global_flag = pending_join_against_sov_event
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = jap.123
	title = jap.123.t
	desc = jap.123.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_officers

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.123.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					is_owned_by = ROOT
					any_neighbor_state = {
						owner = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_owned_state = {
						any_neighbor_state = {
							owner = {
								tag = WJW
								is_puppet_of = JAP
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						owns_state = 613
					}
					WJW = {
						annex_country = {
							target = ROOT
							transfer_troops = yes
						}
						set_capital = { state = 613 }
					}
					else = {
						WJW = {
							annex_country = {
								target = ROOT
								transfer_troops = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_country = {
						limit = {
							is_puppet_of = JAP
							is_neighbor_of = ROOT
						}
						annex_country = {
							target = ROOT
							transfer_troops = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.123.b
		effect_tooltip = {
			JAP = {
				end_puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = wd.1 }
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JAP
			type = topple_government
		}
		JAP = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.124 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = jap.125
	title = jap.125.t
	desc = jap.125.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_asian_politicians

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.123.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claimed_by = ROOT
			}
			add_claim_by = WJW
		}
		WJW = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_idea = KMT_JAP_puppet_no_surrender }}
				add_ideas = KMT_JAP_puppet_no_surrender
			}
			add_manpower = 150000
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_0 amount = 25000 producer = CHI }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = { type = infantry_equipment_1 amount = 2500 producer = JAP }
			annex_country = {
				target = ROOT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = PGR
				}
				WJW = {	
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					country_exists = WJW
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = WJW_established
					}
				}
				WJW = {
					set_country_flag = JAP_puppet
					add_ideas = KMT_jap_military_advisors
					diplomatic_relation = {
						relation = military_access
						country = MAN
						active = yes
					}
				}
				MAN = {
					diplomatic_relation = {
						relation = military_access
						country = WJW
						active = yes
					}
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						is_core_of = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
						OWNER = {
							NOT = { 
								tag = JAP
								is_puppet_of = JAP
							}
						}
					}
					add_claim_by = WJW
				}
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_claimed_by = WJW
							is_core_of = WJW
						}
						controller = {
							OR = {
								tag = JAP
								is_puppet_of = JAP
							}
							NOT = { tag = MEN }
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = {
							any_country = {
								OR = {
									tag = JAP
									is_puppet_of = JAP
								}
								has_full_control_of_state = PREV
							}
						}
						WJW = {
							set_state_controller = PREV
						}
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = WJW_established
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
					OWNER = {
						NOT = { 
							tag = JAP
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
					}
				}
				add_claim_by = WJW
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
			}
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_claimed_by = ROOT
			}
			remove_claim_by = ROOT
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_controlled_by = JAP
					is_core_of = WJW
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						JAP = {
							has_full_control_of_state = PREV
						}
					}
					WJW = {
						set_state_controller = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_global_flag = WJW_established_news
					}
				}
				news_event = { id = jap.126 }
			}
			set_global_flag = WJW_established_news
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			WJW = {
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GAME_OVER_TT
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.123.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		effect_tooltip = {
			JAP = {
				end_puppet = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = wd.1 }
		}
		kill_country_leader = yes
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JAP
			type = topple_government
		}
		JAP = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.124 }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			news_event = { id = jap.127 }
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = jap.128
	hidden = yes
	
	#mean_time_to_happen = { days = 30 }
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = {
		always = no
		has_capitulated = no
		is_puppet_of = JAP
		any_state = {
			owner = { has_war_with = ROOT }
			controller = {
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					is_puppet_of = JAP
				}
			}
			OR = {
				is_core_of = ROOT
				AND = {
					ROOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = WJW
							tag = RGR
							tag = PGR
						}
					}
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				owner = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				controller = {
					NOT = { tag = ROOT }
					OR = {
						tag = JAP
						is_puppet_of = JAP
					}
				}
				OR = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
					is_claimed_by = ROOT
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 621
					controller = {
						tag = MEN
						is_puppet_of = JAP
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					state = 611
					controller = {
						tag = MEN
						is_puppet_of = JAP
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						state = 524
						state = 745
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						OR = {
							tag = JAP
							is_puppet_of = JAP
						}
						has_full_control_of_state = PREV
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					set_state_controller = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
	}
	
}

			has_global_flag = KMT_jap_asked_for_nap
		}
		tag = SOV
		SOV = {
			strength_ratio = {
				tag = JAP
				ratio > 0.5
			}
		}
		OR = {
			is_neighbor_of = JAP
			MAN = {
				is_neighbor_of = SOV
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
			SIK = {
				is_neighbor_of = SOV
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
			MEN = {
				is_neighbor_of = SOV
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
			WJW = {
				is_neighbor_of = SOV
				is_subject_of = JAP
			}
		}
		has_government = communism
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = JAP
			any_country = {
				is_in_faction_with = JAP
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
			any_country = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				has_war_with = JAP
			}
		}

			has_capitulated = no
			NOT = {
				surrender_progress > 0.75
			}
		}

		country_exists = JAP
		OR = {
			AND = {
				GER = {
					has_war_with = FRA
				}
				FRA = {
					has_capitulated = yes
				}
			}
			FRA = {
				OR = {
					exists = no
					is_subject_of = GER
					is_in_faction_with = GER
				}
			}
		}
		any_state = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					tag = SOV
					is_puppet_of = ROOT
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				}
			}
			any_neighbor_state = {
				controller = {
					OR = {
						tag = GER
						is_puppet_of = GER
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
			}
		}
		has_global_flag = GER_JAP_tripartite_pact
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 100 }
	
	option = {
		name = jap.129.a
		ai_chance = { 
			factor = 100
		}
		JAP = {
			country_event = { id = jap.130 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = needs_approval
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			JAP = {				
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = KMT_SOV_JAP_neutrality
					days = 1825
				}
			}
			diplomatic_relation = { country = JAP relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes }
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = KMT_SOV_JAP_neutrality
				days = 1825
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.129.b
	}
}

country_event = {

	is_triggered_only = yes

				}

					country_event = { id = jap.135 hours = 27 }
				}
			}
			every_other_country = {
				limit = { 
					has_war_with = JAP 
					has_volunteers_amount_from = {
						count > 0
						tag = ROOT
					}
				}
				ROOT = { recall_volunteers_from = PREV }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.131.a
		effect_tooltip = {
			SOV = {
				diplomatic_relation = { country = JAP relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes }

					}
				}

				target = ROOT

			}

			has_war_together_with = SOV
			is_in_faction_with = SOV
			is_puppet_of = SOV
		}
		SOV = { 
			surrender_progress > 0.79
			has_war_with = GER 
		}
		has_global_flag = GER_JAP_tripartite_pact
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.138.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SOV
			type = take_state_focus
			generator = { 408 655 409 657 560 563 565 564 566 567 561 }
		}
		GER = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.139 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { has_country_flag = no_help_against_sov}
				}
				add_opinion_modifier = {
					target = ROOT
					modifier = GER_JAP_voracious_opportunitist
				}
			}
		}
		SOV = { country_event = { id = jap.140 }}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		name = jap.138.b
	}
}

		tag = SOV

			has_global_flag = KMT_SOV_had_war_with_JAP
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = JAP
			has_war_with = GER
			has_wargoal_against = JAP
			any_country = {
				is_major = yes
				has_war_with = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 120 }
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				factor = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				surrender_progress > 0.49
				add = -500
			}
		}
		name = jap.141.a
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					tag = JAP
					is_subject_of = JAP
					is_in_faction_with = JAP
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				declare_war_on = {
					target = PREV
					type = topple_government
				}
			}
		}
		JAP = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.142 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					any_country = {
						is_major = yes
						has_war_with = ROOT
					}

			}

country_event = {
	id = jap.152
	title = jap.152.t
	desc = jap.152.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_asian_politicians
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 10}
	
	trigger = {
		tag = JAP
		has_government = fascism
		OR = {
			AND = {
				has_offensive_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				PGR = {
					exists = yes
					has_capitulated = no
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					has_offensive_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				}
				RGR = {
					exists = yes
					has_capitulated = no
					is_subject_of = ROOT
					has_offensive_war_with = event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag
				}
				event_target:KMT_central_gov_tag = {
					surrender_progress > 0.49
				}
			}
			CHI = { exists = no }
		}
		any_state = {
			is_core_of = CHI
			controller = {
				OR = {
					tag = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		CHI = {
			OR = {
				exists = no
				NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = CHI_wang_jingwei ruling_only = yes }}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = { 
		hidden_effect = { 
			random_country = { 
				limit = { has_character = CHI_wang_jingwei }
				CHI_wang_jingwei = { set_nationality = WJW }
				country_event = { id = kmt.722 }
			}
			WJW = { CHI_wang_jingwei = { promote_character = { ideology = pan_asianism }}}
		}
		set_global_flag = KMT_wjw_contacted_jap 
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.152.a
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = jap.156
	title = jap.156.t
	desc = jap.156.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#agree
	option = {
		name = jap.156.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KMT_former_colony_master_hk 
			}
			transfer_state = 326
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KMT_former_colony_master_gzw
			}
			transfer_state = 728
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = KMT_former_colony_master_mc 
			}
			transfer_state = 729
		}
	}
}

#reestablish colonial government rejected
country_event = {
	id = jap.157
	title = jap.157.t
	desc = jap.157.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#do nothing
	option = {
		name = jap.157.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 1
				}
				add = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio < 2
				}
				add = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				tag = FRA
				factor = 100
			}
		}
		add_political_power = -10
	}
	
	#war
	option = {
		name = jap.157.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.5
				}
				add = 20
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 2.25
				}
				add = 25
			}
			modifier = {
				is_major = yes
				add = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				tag = FRA
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = jap.158 }
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = FROM
			type = take_state_focus
			generator = { 326 728 729}
		}
	}
}

## RFP awareness - generic ##
#slip words
country_event = {
	id = jap.159
	title = jap.159.t
	desc = jap.159.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_advisors_remain
	
	trigger = {
		is_subject = yes
		has_country_flag = rfp_path
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event }
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
				days > 30
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
		set_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		days = 125 
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.8
			check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood < 3 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.5
			check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 9 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 100
			check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 14 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.159.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 3 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 14 }
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_add_2_suspicion_tt
		set_temp_variable = { MAN_temp_suspicion = MAN_suspicion }
		add_to_temp_variable = { MAN_temp_suspicion = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MAN_temp_suspicion > 9 }
			}
			set_temp_variable = { MAN_awareness_increase = 1 }
			increase_jap_awareness = yes
			subtract_from_variable = { MAN_suspicion = 10 }
		}else = {
			add_to_variable = { MAN_suspicion = 2 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > -6 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_add_RFP_mood1_tt
			set_temp_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood_increase = -1 }
			add_mood = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.159.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_readinessV > 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_reduce_RFP_str1_tt
			subtract_from_variable = { MAN_RFP_readinessV = 1 }
			else = {
				add_political_power = -50
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_lower_RFP_mood1_tt
		set_temp_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood_increase = 1 }
		add_mood = yes
	}
}

#cell
country_event = {
	id = jap.160
	title = jap.160.t
	desc = {
		text = jap.160.d_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = jap.160.d_2
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavia_partisans
	
	trigger = {
		is_subject = yes
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = MAN_lay_low_flag 
			check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood < 6 }
		}
		awareness_at_least_0 = yes
		check_variable = { MAN_awareness < 15 }
		has_country_flag = rfp_path
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event }
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
						days > 30
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood }
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood
						days > 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood
			set_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
				set_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		days = 100 
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood < 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 9 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -8
				check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 14 }
			}
		}
		name = jap.160.a
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}}
		add_political_power = -50
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_add_RFP_str_tt
		add_to_variable = { MAN_RFP_readinessV = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_add_1_suspicion_tt
		set_temp_variable = { MAN_suspicion_increase = 1 }
		increase_jap_suspicion = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 4 }
			}
		}
		name = jap.160.b
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood < 6 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_add_RFP_mood1_tt
			set_temp_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood_increase = 1 }
			add_mood = yes
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.160.c
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_high_mood_alert_tt
		trigger = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_add_3_suspicion_tt
		set_temp_variable = { MAN_suspicion_increase = 3 }
		increase_jap_suspicion = yes
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = jap.161
	title = jap.161.t
	desc = {
		text = jap.161.d_1
		trigger = {
			NOT = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = jap.161.d_2
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_factory
	
	trigger = {
		is_subject = yes
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = MAN_lay_low_flag 
			check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood < 6 }
		}
		awareness_at_least_0 = yes
		check_variable = { MAN_awareness < 15 }
		has_country_flag = rfp_path
		OR = {
			AND = {
				NOT = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event }
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
						days > 30
					}
				}
			}
			AND = {
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }
				OR = {
					NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood }
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood
						days > 30
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }
			}
			clr_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood
			set_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood
			else = {
				clr_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
				set_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { 
		days = 100 
		modifier = {
			factor = 0.85
			check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood < 5 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.1
			check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 4 }
		}
		modifier = {
			factor = 1.25
			check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 9 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 4 }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 9 }
			}
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}}
		name = jap.161.a
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_add_RFP_str_tt
		add_to_variable = { MAN_RFP_readinessV = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = increase_jap_awareness_tt
		set_temp_variable = { MAN_awareness_increase = 1 }
		increase_jap_awareness = yes
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_add_RFP_mood1_tt
		set_temp_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood_increase = 1 }
		add_mood = yes
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = MAN_nash_put
			days = 30
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		trigger = { NOT = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}}
		name = jap.161.b
		add_political_power = 20
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}
		name = jap.161.c
		add_political_power = -50
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_add_RFP_str_tt
		add_to_variable = { MAN_RFP_readinessV = 1 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = increase_jap_awareness_tt
		set_temp_variable = { MAN_awareness_increase = 1 }
		increase_jap_awareness = yes
	}
}

country_event = {

	title = jap.162.t
	desc = {

		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = jap.162.d_2
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }
		}
	}
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_yugoslavian_cavalry
	
	trigger = {
		is_subject = yes
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = MAN_lay_low_flag 
			check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood < 6 }
		}
		awareness_at_least_0 = yes
		check_variable = { MAN_awareness < 15 }
		has_country_flag = rfp_path

				NOT = { check_variable = { MAN_RFP_mood > 5 }}

						flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
						days > 30
					}

			}

					NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood }
					has_country_flag = {
						flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_mood
						days > 30

				}
			}

			base = 10

			}
		}

#spread manchu nationalistic idea
country_event = {
	id = jap.163
	title = jap.163.t
	desc = jap.163.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_communist_leader
	
	trigger = {
		is_subject = yes
		NOT = { 
			has_country_flag = MAN_lay_low_flag 
		}
		awareness_at_least_0 = yes
		check_variable = { MAN_awareness < 15 }
		has_country_flag = rfp_path
		NOT = {
			has_idea = MAN_nationalistic_sentiment
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event }
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
				days > 60
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
		set_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 125 }
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 9 }
			}
			modifier = {
				add = -5
				check_variable = { MAN_awareness > 14 }
			}
		}
		name = jap.163.a
		add_war_support = 0.01
		add_political_power = 10
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = MAN_nationalistic_sentiment
			days = 60
		}
		set_temp_variable = { MAN_awareness_increase = 1 }
		increase_jap_awareness = yes
	}
	
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		name = jap.163.b
	}
}


### RFP awareness 1 ###
#influx of police
country_event = {
	id = jap.164
	title = jap.164.t
	desc = jap.164.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_communist_leader
	
	trigger = {
		is_subject = yes
		awareness_at_least_1 = yes
		has_country_flag = rfp_path
		NOT = {
			has_idea = MAN_RFP_stay_low
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event }
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
				days > 30
			}
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_stay_low }
			has_country_flag = {
				flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_stay_low
				days > 80
			}
		}
	}
	
	immediate = {
		clr_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
		set_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event
		clr_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_stay_low
		set_country_flag = MAN_rfp_path_event_stay_low
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = { days = 100 }
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		name = jap.164.a
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = MAN_RFP_stay_low
			days = 30
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_stay_low_no_decision_tt
	}
	
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		name = jap.164.b
		random_list = {
			80 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { MAN_RFP_readinessV > 0 }
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_reduce_RFP_str1_tt
					subtract_from_variable = { MAN_RFP_readinessV = 1 }
					else = {
						add_political_power = -50
					}
				}
				set_temp_variable = { MAN_awareness_increase = 1 }
				increase_jap_awareness = yes
			}
			15 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { MAN_RFP_readinessV > 0 }
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_reduce_RFP_str1_tt
					subtract_from_variable = { MAN_RFP_readinessV = 1 }
					else = {
						add_political_power = -50
					}
				}
			}
			5 = {
			}
		}
	}
}

#uphold our bargain
country_event = {
	id = jap.166
	title = jap.166.t
	desc = jap.166.d
	
	picture = GFX_report_event_communist_leader
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	trigger = {
		NOT = { has_global_flag = RFP_refuse_aid }
	}
	
	option = {
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}

#japan demand indochina
country_event = {
	id = jap.193
	title = jap.193.t
	desc = jap.193.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_parade
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.193.a
		trigger = { is_subject = no }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
		}
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.194 }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = ROOT relation = military_access active = yes }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = ROOT relation = docking_rights active = yes }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = ROOT relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes }
		}
		diplomatic_relation = { country = FROM relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_can_occupy_indochina_if_they_have_troops_tt
		set_country_flag = JAP_accepted_indochina_demand
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_indochinese_interest_fired }}
				set_global_flag = JAP_indochinese_interest_fired
				news_event = { id = jap.196 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = IDC_georges_catroux
			}
			retire_character = IDC_georges_catroux
			IDC_jean_decoux = { promote_character = { ideology = oligarchism }}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					OR = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						CONTROLLER = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					}
					has_state_flag = CHI_needed_for_hanoi_route
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = CHI_hanoi_route_closed_state
					}
				}			
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = CHI_needed_for_hanoi_route
						NOT = { has_state_flag = CHI_hanoi_route_closed_state }
						OR = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							CONTROLLER = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = CHI_hanoi_route_closed_state
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				#Country that had the route
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_idea = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea
						has_idea = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea_closed
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = kmt_fsr.10 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = close_hanoi_route_explanation # Prints the contents of the CHI_hanoi_route_current_level variable
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.193.b
		trigger = { is_subject = no }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				any_country = { 
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = FROM
						ratio > 1
					}
				}
				add = 11
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.5
				}
				add = 11
			}
		}
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.195 }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ROOT
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_indochinese_interest_fired }}
				set_global_flag = JAP_indochinese_interest_fired
				news_event = { id = jap.197 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.193.c
		
		trigger = { is_subject = yes }
		if = {
			limit = { is_subject = yes }
			OVERLORD = {
				country_event = { id = jap.268 }
			}
		}else = {
			hidden_effect = {
				FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.271 }}
			}
		}
	}
}

#from botch coup
country_event = {
	id = jap.201
	title = jap.201.t
	desc = jap.201.d
	picture = GFX_report_jap_enter_saigon
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { news_event = { id = jap.209 hours = 2 }}
		if = { limit = { NOT = { country_exists = VIN }} set_country_flag = JAP_no_vin_prior_to_idc_coup }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { country_exists = LAO }} set_country_flag = JAP_no_lao_prior_to_idc_coup }
		if = { limit = { NOT = { country_exists = CAM }} set_country_flag = JAP_no_cam_prior_to_idc_coup }
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAM = {
					OR = { 
						exists = no
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = CAM
				}
				CAM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			IDC = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { 
						is_core_of = CAM
						is_capital = no
					}
					CAM = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				VIN = {
					OR = { 
						exists = no
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = VIN
				}
				VIN = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			IDC = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { 
						is_core_of = VIN
						is_capital = no
					}
					VIN = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				LAO = {
					OR = { 
						exists = no
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = LAO
				}
				LAO = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
			IDC = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = { 
						is_core_of = LAO
						is_capital = no
					}
					LAO = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = JAP_no_vin_prior_to_idc_coup 
				country_exists = VIN
			}
			puppet = VIN
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = JAP_no_lao_prior_to_idc_coup 
				country_exists = LAO
			}
			puppet = LAO
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				has_country_flag = JAP_no_cam_prior_to_idc_coup 
				country_exists = cam
			}
			puppet = CAM
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.201.a
	}
}

#franco thai intervention
country_event = {
	id = jap.211
	title = jap.211.t
	desc = jap.211.d
	picture = GFX_report_franco_thai_war_tank
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.211.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		add_to_variable = { global.JAP_franco_thai_accepted = 1 }
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = jap.212 }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_if_both_agree_franco_thai_tt
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = SIA
					OR = {
						tag = IDC
						is_subject_of = IDC
						is_in_faction_with = IDC
						IDC = { is_subject_of = PREV }
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = SIA
							is_subject_of = SIA
							is_in_faction_with = SIA
							SIA = { is_subject_of = PREV }
						}
					}
					white_peace = PREV
				}
			}
			SIA = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SIA_idc_reparation
					days = 360
				}
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_war_support = 0.2
				add_political_power = 200
			}
			IDC = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 971
							state = 970
							state = 969
						}
					}
					SIA = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IDC_siam_reparation
					days = 360
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { global.JAP_franco_thai_accepted > 1 }}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_war_with = SIA
					OR = {
						tag = IDC
						is_subject_of = IDC
						is_in_faction_with = IDC
						IDC = { is_subject_of = PREV }
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							tag = SIA
							is_subject_of = SIA
							is_in_faction_with = SIA
							SIA = { is_subject_of = PREV }
						}
					}
					white_peace = PREV
				}
			}
			SIA = { 
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = SIA_idc_reparation
					days = 360
				}
				add_stability = 0.1
				add_war_support = 0.2
				add_political_power = 200
			}
			IDC = {
				every_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							state = 971
							state = 970
							state = 969
						}
					}
					SIA = { transfer_state = PREV }
				}
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = IDC_siam_reparation
					days = 360
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.211.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		FROM = {
			country_event = { id = jap.213 }
			add_opinion_modifier = {
				modifier = JAP_no_respect_authority
				target = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { tag = IDC }
			SIA = { country_event = { id = jap.213 }}
		}else = {
			IDC = { country_event = { id = jap.213 }}
		}
	}
}

#MAN ask help response
country_event = {
	id = jap.215
	title = jap.215.t
	desc = {
		text = jap.215.d_1
		trigger = {	
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_resist_communism_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_abolish_monarchy_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_liberal_reform_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_rfp_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_jehol_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_kill_commie_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_special_rights_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_unconditional_flag
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = jap.215.d_2
		trigger = {	
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_resist_communism_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_abolish_monarchy_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_liberal_reform_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_rfp_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_jehol_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_kill_commie_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_special_rights_flag
				}
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = jap.215.d_3
		trigger = {	
			FROM = {
				has_country_flag = MAN_demand_unconditional_flag
			}
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_read_write
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	#accept
	option = {
		name = jap.215.a
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_resist_communism_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_abolish_monarchy_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_liberal_reform_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_rfp_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_jehol_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_kill_commie_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_special_rights_flag
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			FROM = { 
				if = {
					limit = {
						is_in_faction = no
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag
					}
					clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = communism
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = MAN_demand_resist_communism_flag
							has_country_flag = MAN_demand_kill_commie_flag
						}
					}
					clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_resist_communism_flag
					clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_kill_commie_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = fascism
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_rfp_flag
					}
					clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_rfp_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = { NOT = { owns_state = 745 }}
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
					}
					clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = { NOT = { owns_state = 610 }}
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_jehol_flag
					}
					clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_jehol_flag
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						MAN = { NOT = { owns_state = 745 }}
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
					}
					clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
				}
				country_event = { id = jap.217 }
				set_country_flag = MAN_helping_independence
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag 
						is_in_faction = yes
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_demand_faction_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_resist_communism_flag 
						NOT = { has_government = communism }
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_demand_resist_communism_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag 
						is_in_faction = yes
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_demand_faction_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_abolish_monarchy_flag
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_demand_abolish_monarchy_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_liberal_reform_flag
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_demand_liberal_reform_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_rfp_flag 
						NOT = { has_government = fascism }
					}
				}
				set_global_flag = MAN_turned_over_rfp
				if = {
					limit = { has_completed_focus = MAN_contact_russian_fascists }
					uncomplete_national_focus = {
						focus = MAN_contact_russian_fascists
						uncomplete_children = yes
						refund_political_power = no
					}
				}
				SOV = {
					retire_character = SOV_konstantin_rodzayevsky
					hidden_effect = { SOV_konstantin_rodzayevsky = { set_nationality = ZZZ }}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_jehol_flag
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_demand_gib_jehol_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_kill_commie_flag
						NOT = { 
							has_government = communism 
							has_completed_focus = KMT_carry_the_flame
							has_completed_focus = KMT_become_communism
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_demand_kill_commie_tt
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = { 
						has_country_flag = MAN_demand_special_rights_flag
						is_major = yes
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_demand_special_rights_tt
			}
		}else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_from_invalid_help_no_effect_tt
		}
	}
	
	#refuse
	option = {
		name = jap.215.b
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_resist_communism_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_abolish_monarchy_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_liberal_reform_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_rfp_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_jehol_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_kill_commie_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_special_rights_flag
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject = no
				}
			}
			FROM = { 
				country_event = { id = jap.218 }
				clr_country_flag = MAN_helping_independence
				clr_country_flag = MAN_help_response_duration
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_resist_communism_flag
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_abolish_monarchy_flag
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_liberal_reform_flag
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_rfp_flag
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_jehol_flag
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_kill_commie_flag
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_special_rights_flag
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_unconditional_flag
			}
		}else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_from_invalid_help_no_effect_tt
		}
	}
	
	#from refuse
	option = {
		name = jap.215.c
		trigger = {
			FROM = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_faction_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_resist_communism_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_abolish_monarchy_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_liberal_reform_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_rfp_flag
					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag

					has_country_flag = MAN_demand_special_rights_flag

			}
		}

country_event = {

	title = jap.222.t
	desc = jap.222.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty1
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.222.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_in_faction = no
				NOT = {
					any_country = {
						is_subject = no
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
		white_peace = FROM 
		FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.224 }}
	}
	
	option = {
		set_variable = { MAN_PEACE_REJECTED = 0 }
		name = jap.222.c
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		trigger = { 
			is_in_faction = yes 
			any_country = {
				is_subject = no
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				set_variable = { MAN_PEACE_FACTION_INSTANCE@ROOT = 0 }
				set_variable = { MAN_PEACE_AWAITING_RESPONSE@ROOT = 0 }
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				OR = {
					is_subject = no
					has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				}
			}
			set_variable = { MAN_PEACE_FACTION_INSTANCE@ROOT = 1 }
			set_variable = { MAN_PEACE_AWAITING_RESPONSE@ROOT = 1 }
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				OR = {
					is_subject = no
					has_autonomy_state = autonomy_dominion
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = jap.223 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.222.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_country_flag = MAN_helping_independence }
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.225 }}
	}
}

	desc = jap.223.d

			limit = {
				NOT = {
					any_country = {
						NOT = { tag = ROOT }
						check_variable = { MAN_PEACE_FACTION_INSTANCE@FROM = 1 }
						check_variable = { MAN_PEACE_AWAITING_RESPONSE@FROM = 1 }
					}
				}
				FROM = { check_variable = { KMT_WD_PEACE_REJECTED@FROM.FROM = 1 }}
			}
			FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.226 }}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { check_variable = { FROM.MAN_peace_counter = 0 }}
				FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.226 }}
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.222.b
		set_variable = { MAN_PEACE_AWAITING_RESPONSE@FROM = 0 }
		set_variable = { FROM.MAN_PEACE_REJECTED = 0 }
		FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.227 }}
	}
}

			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = neutrality
			popularity = 0.05
		}

			ideology = fascism
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		clr_country_flag = MAN_soc_party
		clr_country_flag = MAN_lib_party
		set_country_flag = MAN_con_party
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic name = MAN_imperial_conservative_party long_name = MAN_imperial_conservative_party_long }
	}

		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		clr_country_flag = MAN_soc_party
		set_country_flag = MAN_lib_party
		clr_country_flag = MAN_con_party
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic name = MAN_imperial_liberal_party long_name = MAN_imperial_liberal_party_long }
	}
	
	#soc

		name = jap.237.c
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = democratic
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {

		clr_country_flag = MAN_con_party

	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.242.a
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.229 }
			transfer_state = 745

			every_country = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag }
				add_opinion_modifier = { target = ROOT modifier = MAN_no_dairen }
				clr_country_flag = MAN_demand_gib_dairen_flag
				country_event = { id = jap.231 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	#no

	}
}

#MAN seek peace
country_event = {
	id = jap.248
	title = jap.248.t
	desc = jap.248.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = jap.248.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		white_peace = FROM
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				OWNER = {
					OR = {
						tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				CONTROLLER = {
					OR = {
						tag = FROM
						is_subject_of = FROM
						is_in_faction_with = FROM
						tag = ROOT
						is_subject_of = ROOT
						is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					}
				}
				OR = {
					region = 155
					region = 242
					region = 243
				}
			}
			FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = MAN_korean_cooperation_flag
				KOR = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = FROM
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					CONTROLLER = {
						OR = {
							tag = FROM
							is_subject_of = FROM
							is_in_faction_with = FROM
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					OR = {
						region = 186
					}
				}
				KOR = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}else = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					OWNER = {
						OR = {
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					CONTROLLER = {
						OR = {
							tag = FROM
							is_subject_of = FROM
							is_in_faction_with = FROM
							tag = ROOT
							is_subject_of = ROOT
							is_in_faction_with = ROOT
						}
					}
					OR = {
						region = 186
					}
				}
				FROM = { transfer_state = PREV }
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.249 }}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.248.b
		FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.250 }}
	}
}
