#jap demo coup
country_event = {
	id = jap.251
	title = jap.251.t
	desc = jap.251.d
	
	picture = GFX_gen
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	fire_only_once = yes
	
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 745 = { OWNER = { original_tag = JAP }}}
				transfer_state = 745
				add_state_core = 745
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						original_tag = JAP
						MEN = { is_subject_of = PREV }
					}
				}
				MAN = { puppet = MEN }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						original_tag = JAP
						ECR = { is_subject_of = PREV }
					}
				}
				MAN = { puppet = ECR }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					any_country = {
						original_tag = JAP
						EHA = { is_subject_of = PREV }
					}
				}
				MAN = { puppet = EHA }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.251.a
		trigger = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = MAN_an_alternative }}
		set_cosmetic_tag = MAN_kwantung_army
		if = {
			limit = {
				MAN = { has_idea = MAN_reliant_idea }
			}
			MAN = { remove_ideas = MAN_reliant_idea }
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = MAN_more_japanese_immigrants
		add_to_variable = { MAN_japanese_immigrants_number = 1000 }
		set_country_flag = MAN_kwantung_terr_flag
		MAN_kwantung_army = { 
			set_portraits = {
				civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/kwantung_army_leader.tga" }
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					traits = { MAN_kwantung_army_trait }
					expire = "1965.1.1"
					ideology = fascism_ideology
				}
			}
		}
		#load_focus_tree = {
		#	tree = KTA_focus
		#	keep_completed = no
		#}
		load_focus_tree = {
			tree = KTA_focus
			keep_completed = no
		}
		MAN_swap_out_japanese_traits = yes
	}
	
	option = {
		trigger = { NOT = { has_completed_focus = MAN_enhance_local_policing }}
		name = jap.251.b
		start_civil_war = {
			ruling_party = neutrality
			ideology = fascism
			size = 0.5
			keep_unit_leaders_trigger = { always = yes }
			states_filter = { NOT = { has_state_flag = MAN_state_secured }}
			if = {
				limit = { ECR = { is_subject_of = ROOT }}
				puppet = ECR
			}
			if = {
				limit = { EHA = { is_subject_of = ROOT }}
				puppet = EHA
			}
			if = {
				limit = { MEN = { is_subject_of = ROOT }}
				puppet = MEN
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = MAN_kwantung_army
			set_country_flag = MAN_kwantung_terr_flag
			load_focus_tree = {
				tree = KTA_focus
				keep_completed = no
			}
		}
		random_country = {
			limit = { 
				original_tag = ROOT
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
			}
			ROOT = {
				every_character = { 
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = MAN_is_japanese_character 
							has_character_flag = JAP_true_jap_characters 
						}
					}
					set_nationality = PREV.PREV
				}
				transfer_units_fraction = {
					size = 0
					navy_ratio = 0.9
				}
			}
			MAN_swap_out_japanese_traits = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					MAN = { has_idea = MAN_reliant_idea }
				}
				MAN = { remove_ideas = MAN_reliant_idea }
			}
			set_party_name = { ideology = fascism name = MAN_kantogun_party }
			MAN_kwantung_army = { 
				set_portraits = {
					civilian = { large = "gfx/leaders/kmt_mod/kwantung_army_leader.tga" }
				}
				add_country_leader_role = {
					promote_leader = yes
					country_leader = {
						traits = { MAN_kwantung_army_trait }
						expire = "1965.1.1"
						ideology = fascism_ideology
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

			if = {
				limit = { WJW = { is_subject_of = ROOT }}
				WJW = { transfer_state = 729 }
			}else = {
				transfer_state = 729
			}
			FROM.FROM = { add_state_claim = 729 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.253.a
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_political_power = 100
		effect_tooltip = {
			if = {
				limit = { WJW = { is_subject_of = ROOT }}
				WJW = { transfer_state = 729 }
			}else = {
				transfer_state = 729
			}
			FROM.FROM = { add_state_claim = 729 }
		}
	}
}

	id = jap.268

	desc = jap.193.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_japanese_parade
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.193.a
		trigger = { is_subject = no }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
		}
		JAP = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.194 }
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				OR = { 
					tag = ROOT
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
				any_owned_state = { 
					region = 142
					NOT = { state = 289 }
				}
			}
			JAP = {
				diplomatic_relation = { country = PREV relation = military_access active = yes }
				diplomatic_relation = { country = PREV relation = docking_rights active = yes }
				diplomatic_relation = { country = PREV relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes }
				diplomatic_relation = { country = PREV relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes }
			}
			set_country_flag = JAP_accepted_indochina_demand
		}
		diplomatic_relation = { country = JAP relation = non_aggression_pact active = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = JAP_can_occupy_indochina_if_they_have_troops_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_indochinese_interest_fired }}
				set_global_flag = JAP_indochinese_interest_fired
				news_event = { id = jap.196 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_character = IDC_georges_catroux
			}
			retire_character = IDC_georges_catroux
			IDC_jean_decoux = { promote_character = { ideology = oligarchism }}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				any_state = {
					OR = {
						is_controlled_by = ROOT
						CONTROLLER = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
					}
					has_state_flag = CHI_needed_for_hanoi_route
					NOT = {
						has_state_flag = CHI_hanoi_route_closed_state
					}
				}			
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_state = {
					limit = {
						has_state_flag = CHI_needed_for_hanoi_route
						NOT = { has_state_flag = CHI_hanoi_route_closed_state }
						OR = {
							is_controlled_by = ROOT
							CONTROLLER = { is_subject_of = ROOT }
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = CHI_hanoi_route_closed_state
				}
			}
			random_country = {
				#Country that had the route
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						has_idea = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea
						has_idea = KMT_yunnan_bahn_idea_closed
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = kmt_fsr.10 }
				custom_effect_tooltip = close_hanoi_route_explanation # Prints the contents of the CHI_hanoi_route_current_level variable
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.269 }}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.193.b
		trigger = { is_subject = no }
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				any_country = { 
					is_in_faction_with = ROOT
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = FROM
						ratio > 1
					}
				}
				add = 11
			}
			modifier = {
				strength_ratio = {
					tag = FROM
					ratio > 1.5
				}
				add = 11
			}
		}
		JAP = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.195 }
			create_wargoal = {
				target = ROOT
				type = puppet_wargoal_focus
			}
		}
		FROM = { country_event = { id = jap.270 }}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { has_global_flag = JAP_indochinese_interest_fired }}
				set_global_flag = JAP_indochinese_interest_fired
				news_event = { id = jap.197 }
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = jap.276.d

	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	immediate = {
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.276.a
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 5 
			modifier = { 
				FROM = { is_ai = no	}
				add = 15
			}
			modifier = { 
				FROM = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 0.5
					}
				}
				add = 5
			}
			modifier = { 
				FROM = {
					strength_ratio = {
						tag = ROOT
						ratio > 1
					}
				}
				add = 25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { 
				OR = {
					owns_state = 609 
					owns_state = 608 
				}
			}
			every_owned_state = {
				limit = { 
					OR = {
						state = 608
						state = 609
					}
				}
				FROM = { 
					transfer_state = PREV
				}
			}
			FROM = { 
				country_event = { id = jap.277 }
			}
		}
		every_other_country = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { tag = FROM }
				NOT = { tag = ROOT }
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				OR = {
					owns_state = 609 
					owns_state = 608 
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = jap.279 }
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = jap.276.b
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 10 
			modifier = { 
				FROM = { is_ai = no }
				factor = 0.1
			}
		}
		FROM = { 
			country_event = { id = jap.278 }
		}
	}
}
